<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Alcon Reports Solid Financial Results for Second Quarter</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Second Quarter Highlights</font></font></div>
<div>

<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;&#160;&#160;</font></div></td>
<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Organic sales growth was 3.3 percent in second quarter (-3.4 percent reported)</font></div></td></tr></table></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Cost management programs contributed to earnings per share of $1.94</font></div></td></tr></table></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<td align="right" style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;&#160;&#160;</font></div></td>
<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Operational leverage continued as earnings per share rose 3.2&#160;&#160;percent</font></div></td></tr></table></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td align="right" style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;&#160;&#160;</font></div></td>
<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Management raises full year earnings per share guidance</font></div></td></tr></table></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">HUENENBERG, Switzerland &#8211; July 22, 2009 &#8211; </font>Alcon, Inc. (NYSE:ACL) reported global sales of $1,677 million for the second quarter of 2009, a 3.3 percent increase excluding the impact of foreign exchange fluctuations, or a decrease of 3.4 percent compared to the second quarter
of 2008 on a reported basis. Net earnings for the second quarter of 2009 rose 2.6 percent to $582 million, or $1.94 per diluted share, compared to $567 million, or $1.88 per diluted share, in the second quarter of 2008.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8220;Organic sales growth is coming in as expected in 2009, as we continue to execute our sales and marketing strategies that allow us to grow even in the face of global economic weakness,&#8221; said Kevin Buehler, Alcon&#8217;s president and chief executive officer. &#8220;We expect that further development of key businesses like glaucoma,
advanced technology intraocular lenses and emerging markets will enable us to achieve our full year guidance of mid-single digit organic sales growth with somewhat higher organic growth in the second half of the year than in the first, and to translate that growth into solid earnings performance.&#8221;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Sales Highlights</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Summarized below are the key drivers of sales in the second quarter of 2009.&#160;&#160;All growth comparisons are for the second quarter of 2009 compared to the second quarter of 2008.&#160;&#160;Organic sales growth rates exclude currency impacts and acquisitions and are non-GAAP measures that are reconciled in a table at the end of this
release.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td align="right" style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Wingdings">&#216;&#160;&#160;</font></div></td>
<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">International organic sales growth was 5.9 percent (-6.4 percent reported), with emerging markets rising 8.1 percent organically (-8.2 percent reported).</font></div></td></tr></table></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">

<td align="right" style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Wingdings">&#216;&#160;&#160;</font></div></td>
<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">U.S. sales stabilized as they increased 0.3 percent due to strong contributions from advanced technology <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">AcrySof</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> intraocular lenses and share gains and market growth in glaucoma offset by generic
competition to <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">TobraDex</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> ophthalmic suspension.</font></div></td></tr></table></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td align="right" style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Wingdings">&#216;&#160;&#160;</font></div></td>
<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Advanced technology intraocular lenses rose 38.3 percent organically, (+30.1 percent reported) due to market share gains by the <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">AcrySof</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"> ReSTOR</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Aspheric
+3.0 </font>lens, which was launched in the United States in January of 2009, and the continued rapid adoption of <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">AcrySof</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"> IQ Toric</font> by cataract surgeons.</font></div></td></tr></table></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">

<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Glaucoma sales rose 16.6 percent organically (+8.3 percent reported) led by a 23.6 percent organic rise (+15.4 percent reported) in global sales of <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">TRAVATAN</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">,
TRAVATAN Z</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> and <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">DuoTrav</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">TM</font> ophthalmic solutions, as these products continued global market share growth in the prostaglandin category.&#160;&#160;The launch of <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Azarga</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174; </font>ophthalmic
solution in the European Union contributed to unit growth of 15.5 percent for the <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Azopt</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">/Azarga</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> family.</font></div></td></tr></table></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td align="right" style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Wingdings">&#216;&#160;&#160;</font></div></td>
<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Sales of allergy products declined 1.8 percent organically (-4.8 percent reported), consistent with the company&#8217;s expectations for a weaker spring allergy market in the United States.&#160;&#160;The company increased combined <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Patanol</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> and <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Pataday</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#8482;</font> ophthalmic
solutions U.S. market share to 78.6 percent May year-to-date, an improvement of 0.8 percent over the prior year.</font></div></td></tr></table></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Earnings Highlights</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Summarized below are the key drivers of earnings in the second quarter of 2009.&#160;&#160;All growth comparisons are for the second quarter of 2009 compared to the second quarter of 2008.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td align="right" style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Wingdings">&#216;&#160;&#160;</font></div></td>
<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Operating income margin rose from 37.2 to 37.7 percent of sales and net income margin increased from 32.6 percent to 34.7 percent of sales.</font></div></td></tr></table></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td align="right" style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Wingdings">&#216;&#160;&#160;</font></div></td>
<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Cost management programs and foreign exchange fluctuations led to a sharp reduction in selling general and administrative expenses from 30.4 to 27.9 percent of sales.</font></div></td></tr></table></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td align="right" style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Wingdings">&#216;&#160;&#160;</font></div></td>
<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Other income in the second quarter of 2009 was $19 million compared to $4 million in the second quarter of 2008, due primarily to gains from foreign currency transactions.</font></div></td></tr></table></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td align="right" style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Wingdings">&#216;&#160;&#160;</font></div></td>
<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The effective tax rate for the second quarter of 2009 was 10.6 percent, which included approximately one percentage point of period benefits related to settlement with tax authorities on prior year taxes.</font></div></td></tr></table></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Other Highlights</font></div>
<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td align="right" style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Wingdings">&#216;&#160;&#160;</font></div></td>
<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Alcon has entered into a five-year collaborative research agreement with AstraZeneca for the exclusive ophthalmic discovery and potential development rights to AstraZeneca&#8217;s compound library.&#160;&#160;The agreement covers multiple classes of small molecules with lead compounds targeting development of drugs to treat sight-threatening conditions
such as glaucoma, wet and dry age-related macular degeneration and other retinal diseases, as well as ocular allergy, dry eye and other inflammatory eye conditions.</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div></td></tr></table></div>
<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td align="right" style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Wingdings">&#216;&#160;&#160;</font></div></td>
<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Alcon has entered into a research and licensing agreement with PhiloGene, Inc. for rights to a VEGF protein.&#160;&#160;The company plans to develop this protein for the treatment of wet age related macular degeneration and diabetic macular edema.</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div></td></tr></table></div>

system that enhances bioavailability to targeted tissues.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Alcon completed the European Union decentralized registration procedure for <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Vigamox</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174; </font>ophthalmic solution.<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#160;</font>National licenses have been
issued by Bulgaria, Iceland and Romania and the company is awaiting licensing from the remaining 23 countries.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Financial Guidance</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The company reaffirmed its previously-issued sales guidance for&#160;full year 2009 organic sales growth to be in the mid-single digits.&#160;&#160;The company raised its guidance for full year 2009 diluted earnings per share on a U.S. GAAP basis to between $6.20 and $6.35 and between $6.25 and $6.40 on a non-GAAP adjusted basis (excluding
restructuring charges taken in the first half of 2009).&#160;&#160;This increase reflects positive earnings performance in the first half of the year, which is expected to be partially mitigated by higher R&amp;D and SG&amp;A expenses in the second half of the year.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">About Alcon</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Alcon, Inc. is the world&#8217;s leading eye care company, with sales of approximately $6.3 billion in 2008.&#160;&#160;Alcon, which has been dedicated to the ophthalmic industry for 65 years, researches, develops, manufactures and markets pharmaceuticals, surgical equipment and devices, contacts lens solutions and other vision care products
that treat diseases, disorders and other conditions of the eye.&#160;&#160;Alcon operates in 75 countries and sells products in 180 markets. Alcon&#8217;s majority shareholder is Nestl&#233;, S.A., the world&#8217;s largest food company.&#160;&#160;For more information on Alcon, Inc., visit the Company&#8217;s web site at <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">www.alcon.com</font>.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">N/M - Not Meaningful</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Note: Organic change calculates sales growth without the impact of foreign exchange fluctuations and acquisitions. Management believes organic sales change is an important measure of the company&#8217;s operations because it provides investors with a clearer picture of the core rate of sales growth due to changes in unit volumes and local
currency prices.&#160;&#160;This measure is considered a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by Regulation G promulgated by the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission.&#160;&#160;Certain reclassifications have been made to prior year amounts to conform to current year presentation.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">N/M - Not Meaningful</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Note: Organic change calculates sales growth without the impact of foreign exchange fluctuations and acquisitions. Management believes organic sales change is an important measure of the company&#8217;s operations because it provides investors with a clearer picture of the core rate of sales growth due to changes in unit volumes and local
currency prices.&#160;&#160;This measure is considered a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by Regulation G promulgated by the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission.&#160;&#160;Certain reclassifications have been made to prior year amounts to conform to current year presentation.</font></div>
